   9              	;@"     This sourcecode is released for the purpose to promote programming  "
  10              	;@"  on the Raspberry Pi. You may redistribute it and/or modify with the    "

  12              	;@"																            "
  13              	;@"      The SOURCE CODE is distributed "AS IS" WITHOUT WARRANTIES AS TO    "
  14              	;@"   PERFORMANCE OF MERCHANTABILITY WHETHER EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED.          "
  15              	;@"   Redistributions of source code must retain the copyright notices to   "
  16              	;@"   maintain the author credit (attribution) .							"
  17              	;@"																			"
  18              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  19              	;@"                                                                         "
  20              	;@"       This code expands on my earlier SmartStart bootstub assembler for "
  21              	;@" the Pi 1/2/3. It simplifies some of the autodetect code but importantly "
  22              	;@" directly supports multicore operation in C/C++. To do that it provides  "
  23              	;@" stack space to each core and provides a modified bootloader spinlock    "
  24              	;@" that protects against registers R0-R3 trashed. As any C/C++ compiler    "
  25              	;@" code will trash those registers, to use C/C++ in multicore programming  "
  26              	;@" this protection must be done.											"
  27              	;@"      The downside is this bootstub must be a little more complex in     "
  28              	;@" that it must start and setup multiple cores. The code is much more      "
  29              	;@" connected to the linker file which provides memory space to each core.  "
  30              	;@"       There is however matching paired AARCH64 stub and linker files    "
  31              	;@" so code written for this setup can be ported to AARCH64 with ease.		"
  32              	;@"																            "
  33              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++[ REVISIONS ]+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"
  34              	;@"  1.01 Initial release .. Pi autodetection main aim                      "
  35              	;@"  1.02 Many functions moved out C to aide 32/64 bit compatability        "
  36              	;@"  2.01 Futher reductions to bare minmum assembeler code                  "
  37              	;@"  2.02 Multicore functionality added                                     "
  38              	;@"  2.03 Timer Irq support added  											"
  39              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"*/
  40              	
  41              	;@"========================================================================="
  42              	;@"				 	 ARM CPU ID CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    "
  43              	;@"========================================================================="
  44              	.equ ARM6_CPU_ID, 0x410FB767					;@ CPU id a BCM2835 reports
  45              	.equ ARM7_CPU_ID, 0x410FC073					;@ CPU id a BCM2836 reports
  46              	.equ ARM8_CPU_ID, 0x410FD034					;@ CPU id a BCM2837 reports
  47              	
  48              	;@"========================================================================="
  49              	;@"				 	 ARM CPU MODE CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    "
  50              	;@"========================================================================="
  51              	.equ CPU_FIQMODE, 0x11							;@ CPU in FIQ mode
  52              	.equ CPU_IRQMODE, 0x12							;@ CPU in IRQ mode
  53              	.equ CPU_SVCMODE, 0x13							;@ CPU in SVC mode
  54              	.equ CPU_HYPMODE, 0x1A							;@ CPU in HYP mode
ARM GAS  C:\Users\ldebo\AppData\Local\Temp\ccISOhOE.s 			page 2


  55              	
  56              	;@"========================================================================="
  57              	;@"				 ARM CPU IRQ/FIQ BIT CONSTANT DEFINITIONS				    "
  58              	;@"========================================================================="
  59              	#define I_Bit  (1 << 7)							// Irq flag bit in cpsr (CPUMODE register)
  60              	#define F_Bit  (1 << 6)							// Fiq flag bit in cpsr (CPUMODE register)
  61              	
  62              	;@"========================================================================="
  63              	;@"				 	 ARM CPU MODE CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    "
  64              	;@"========================================================================="
  65              	.equ CPU_FIQMODE_VALUE, (CPU_FIQMODE | I_Bit | F_Bit)	;@ CPU in FIQ mode with irq, fiq off
  66              	.equ CPU_IRQMODE_VALUE, (CPU_IRQMODE | I_Bit | F_Bit)	;@ CPU in IRQ mode with irq, fiq off
  67              	.equ CPU_SVCMODE_VALUE, (CPU_SVCMODE | I_Bit | F_Bit)	;@ CPU in SVC mode with irq, fiq off
  68

  90              	_start:
  91              	;@"================================================================"
  92              	;@ Grab cpu mode and start address and hold in a high register.
  93              	;@"================================================================"
  94 0000 0FC0A0E1 		mov r12, pc;							;@ Hold boot address in high register R12
  95 0004 00B00FE1 		mrs r11, CPSR							;@ Read current CPU mode
  96 0008 1FB00BE2 		and r11, r11, #0x1F						;@ Clear all but CPU mode bits in register r11
  97              	;@"================================================================"
  98              	;@ If the cpu is in HYP_MODE(EL2) we will bring it SVC_MODE (EL1).
  99              	;@"================================================================"
 100              	multicore_start:
 101 000c 00000FE1 	    mrs r0,cpsr								;@ Fetch the cpsr register which includes CPU mode bits 
 102 0010 1F1000E2 	 	and r1, r0, #0x1F						;@ Mask off the CPU mode bits to register r1                            
 103 0014 1A0051E3 	 	cmp r1, #CPU_HYPMODE					;@ Check we are in HYP_MODE											
 104 0018 0500001A 		bne .NotInHypMode						;@ Branch if not equal meaning was not in HYP_MODE  
 105 001c 1F00C0E3 		bic r0,r0,#0x1F							;@ Clear the CPU mode bits in register r0							
 106 0020 D30080E3 		orr r0, r0, #CPU_SVCMODE_VALUE			;@ SVC_MODE bits onto register with Irq/Fiq disabled	
 107 0024 00F06FE1 	    msr spsr_cxsf,r0						;@ Hold value in spsr_cxsf
 108 0028 04E08FE2 	    add lr,pc,#4							;@ Calculate address of .NotInHypMode label
 109              		/* I borrowed this trick from Ultibo because ARM6 code running on an ARM7/8 needs this opcode  */
 110              		/* The ARM6 compiler does not know these instructions so it is a way to get needed opcode here */
 111              	    /* So our ARM6 code can drop an arm7 or arm8 out of HYP mode and run on an ARM7/8.

 112              	 	/* Native ARM7/8 compilers already understand the OPCODE but do not mind it this way either	   */

 114 0030 6E0060E1 		.long 0xE160006E						;@ "eret" Elevated return which will exit at .NotInHypMode in SVC_MODE
 115              	.NotInHypMode:

 119 0034 4C229FE5 	    ldr r2, = __SVC_stack_core0				;@ Address of svc_stack_core0 stack pointer value

 142              	set_svc_stack:
 143 0090 02D0A0E1 		mov sp, r2								;@ Set the stack pointer for SVC_MODE
